const COLORS = {
  'Planejamento': '#64748b',
  'Licitação': '#f59e0b',
  'Empenho': '#8b5cf6',
  'Execução': '#3b82f6',
  'Concluída': '#10b981',
  'Concluída Parcial': '#34d399',
  'Cancelada': '#ef4444',
  'Outros': '#374151'
};

const PLT = {
  paper: 'rgba(0,0,0,0)',
  plot: 'rgba(0,0,0,0)',
  font: { color: '#94a3b8', family: 'DM Sans' },
  grid: '#1e293b'
};

function plotLayout(extra) {
  return Object.assign({
    paper_bgcolor: PLT.paper, plot_bgcolor: PLT.plot,
    font: PLT.font, margin: { t:20, b:40, l:40, r:20 },
    xaxis: { gridcolor: PLT.grid, zerolinecolor: PLT.grid },
    yaxis: { gridcolor: PLT.grid, zerolinecolor: PLT.grid },
    showlegend: false
  }, extra);
}

function fmt(v) {
  if(v >= 1e6) return 'R$ ' + (v/1e6).toFixed(1) + 'M';
  return 'R$ ' + (v/1e3).toFixed(0) + 'K';
}

function showPage(id) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.page').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(n => n.classList.remove('active'));
  document.getElementById('page-' + id).classList.add('active');
  document.querySelector(`[onclick="showPage('${id}')"]`).classList.add('active');
  renderPage(id);
}

const rendered = {};
function renderPage(id) {
  if(rendered[id]) return;
  rendered[id] = true;

  if(id === 'overview') renderOverview();
  if(id === 'pipeline') renderPipeline();
  if(id === 'vereadores') renderVereadores();
  if(id === 'secretarias') renderSecretarias();
  if(id === 'tipos') renderTipos();
  if(id === 'explorador') renderExplorador();
}

function renderOverview() {

  // Tipos pie
  Plotly.newPlot('chart-tipos-pie', [
    { type:'pie', labels: tipoData.map(d=>d.Tipo.replace('E CONTRATAÇÕES ARTÍSTICAS','').replace('E PROJETOS SOCIAIS','')),
       values: tipoData.map(d=>d.valor),
       hole: 0.45,
       marker:{ colors:['#3b82f6','#10b981','#f59e0b','#8b5cf6','#ef4444','#06b6d4'] },
       textinfo:'percent', hovertemplate:'%{label}<br>%{value:,.0f}<extra></extra>'
    }
  ], plotLayout({ showlegend:true, legend:{orientation:'v', x:1.05, y:0.5, font:{size:10}} }), {responsive:true});



  // Secretarias
  const top10sec = secData.slice(0,10);
  Plotly.newPlot('chart-sec-bar', [
    { type:'bar', orientation:'h',
       y: top10sec.map(d=>d.Secretaria_curta.length > 25 ? d.Secretaria_curta.slice(0,25)+'…' : d.Secretaria_curta).reverse(),
       x: top10sec.map(d=>d.valor).reverse(),
       marker:{ color:'#10b981', opacity:0.85 },
       hovertemplate:'%{y}: R$ %{x:,.0f}<extra></extra>'
    }
  ], plotLayout({ margin:{l:160,r:60,t:10,b:30} }), {responsive:true});
}

function renderPipeline() {
  // Main pipeline chart (horizontal bar stacked)
  const fasesOrdem = ['Planejamento','Licitação','Empenho','Execução','Concluída','Concluída Parcial','Cancelada'];
  const fases = fasesOrdem.map(f => faseData.find(d=>d.Fase===f)).filter(Boolean);
  
  Plotly.newPlot('chart-pipeline', [
    { type:'bar', orientation:'h',
       y: fases.map(d=>d.Fase).reverse(),
       x: fases.map(d=>d.valor).reverse(),
       marker:{ color: fases.map(d=>COLORS[d.Fase]||'#64748b').reverse() },
       text: fases.map(d=>fmt(d.valor)+' ('+d.qtd+')').reverse(),
       textposition:'outside',
       hovertemplate:'%{y}<br>R$ %{x:,.0f}<extra></extra>'
    }
  ], plotLayout({ margin:{l:140,r:120,t:20,b:30} }), {responsive:true});

  // Qtd por fase
  Plotly.newPlot('chart-fase-qtd', [
    { type:'bar', x: fases.map(d=>d.Fase), y: fases.map(d=>d.qtd),
       marker:{ color: fases.map(d=>COLORS[d.Fase]||'#64748b') },
       text: fases.map(d=>d.qtd), textposition:'outside',
       hovertemplate:'%{x}: %{y}<extra></extra>'
    }
  ], plotLayout({ margin:{l:40,r:20,t:20,b:80}, xaxis:{tickangle:-30} }), {responsive:true});

  // Avg por fase
  Plotly.newPlot('chart-fase-avg', [
    { type:'bar', x: fases.map(d=>d.Fase), y: fases.map(d=>d.qtd>0?d.valor/d.qtd:0),
       marker:{ color: fases.map(d=>COLORS[d.Fase]||'#64748b') },
       text: fases.map(d=>fmt(d.qtd>0?d.valor/d.qtd:0)), textposition:'outside',
       hovertemplate:'%{x}: R$ %{y:,.0f}<extra></extra>'
    }
  ], plotLayout({ margin:{l:40,r:20,t:20,b:80}, xaxis:{tickangle:-30} }), {responsive:true});
}

function renderVereadores() {
  // Grouped bar: total vs concluido
  const v20 = verData.slice(0,20);
  Plotly.newPlot('chart-ver-efic', [
    { type:'bar', name:'Total', orientation:'h',
       y: v20.map(d=>d.Vereador).reverse(), x: v20.map(d=>d.total).reverse(),
       marker:{ color:'rgba(59,130,246,0.4)' }, hovertemplate:'%{y} total: R$ %{x:,.0f}<extra></extra>'
    },
    { type:'bar', name:'Concluído', orientation:'h',
       y: v20.map(d=>d.Vereador).reverse(), x: v20.map(d=>d.concluido).reverse(),
       marker:{ color:'#10b981' }, hovertemplate:'%{y} concluído: R$ %{x:,.0f}<extra></extra>'
    }
  ], plotLayout({ barmode:'overlay', showlegend:true, legend:{orientation:'h',x:0,y:1.05},
     margin:{l:200,r:80,t:40,b:30} }), {responsive:true});

  // Table
  const tbody = document.getElementById('ver-tbody');
  tbody.innerHTML = verData.slice(0,30).map((d,i)=>{
    const eficColor = d.efic >= 80 ? '#10b981' : d.efic >= 50 ? '#f59e0b' : '#ef4444';
    return `<tr>
      <td class="rank-num">${i+1}</td>
      <td><strong>${d.Vereador}</strong></td>
      <td class="font-mono">${fmt(d.total)}</td>
      <td class="font-mono" style="color:#34d399">${fmt(d.concluido)}</td>
      <td>${d.qtd}</td>
      <td>
        <div style="color:${eficColor};font-weight:600;font-size:0.8rem">${d.efic}%</div>
        <div class="efic-bar"><div class="efic-fill" style="width:${d.efic}%;background:${eficColor}"></div></div>
      </td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join('');
}

function renderSecretarias() {
  Plotly.newPlot('chart-sec-full', [
    { type:'bar', orientation:'h',
       y: secData.map(d=>d.Secretaria_curta.length>35?d.Secretaria_curta.slice(0,35)+'…':d.Secretaria_curta).reverse(),
       x: secData.map(d=>d.valor).reverse(),
       marker:{ color:'#06b6d4', opacity:0.85 },
       text: secData.map(d=>fmt(d.valor)+' ('+d.qtd+')').reverse(),
       textposition:'outside', hovertemplate:'%{y}: R$ %{x:,.0f}<extra></extra>'
    }
  ], plotLayout({ margin:{l:200,r:120,t:20,b:30} }), {responsive:true});
}

function renderTipos() {
  Plotly.newPlot('chart-tipo-bar', [
    { type:'bar', orientation:'h',
       y: tipoData.map(d=>d.Tipo).reverse(), x: tipoData.map(d=>d.valor).reverse(),
       marker:{ color:['#3b82f6','#10b981','#f59e0b','#8b5cf6','#ef4444','#06b6d4'].reverse() },
       text: tipoData.map(d=>fmt(d.valor)).reverse(), textposition:'outside',
       hovertemplate:'%{y}: R$ %{x:,.0f}<extra></extra>'
    }
  ], plotLayout({ margin:{l:220,r:100,t:10,b:30} }), {responsive:true});

  Plotly.newPlot('chart-tipo-pie', [
    { type:'pie',
       labels: tipoData.map(d=>d.Tipo), values: tipoData.map(d=>d.qtd),
       hole:0.4, marker:{ colors:['#3b82f6','#10b981','#f59e0b','#8b5cf6','#ef4444','#06b6d4'] },
       textinfo:'percent+label', hovertemplate:'%{label}: %{value} emendas<extra></extra>'
    }
  ], plotLayout({ showlegend:false, margin:{l:10,r:10,t:10,b:10} }), {responsive:true});
}

let dtTable = null;
let currentFase = 'Todos';
function renderExplorador() {
  const cleanData = rawData.filter(d => d.Fase !== 'Outros' && d.Vereador && !d.Vereador.startsWith('*') && d.Valor > 0);
  dtTable = $('#mainTable').DataTable({
    data: cleanData,
    columns: [
      { data:'Vereador' },
      { data:'Objeto', defaultContent:'' },
      { data:'Tipo', defaultContent:'' },
      { data:'Secretaria', defaultContent:'' },
      { data:'Fase', render: d => `<span class="fase-badge fase-${d}">${d}</span>` },
      { data:'Valor', render: v => '<span class="font-mono">' + (v||0).toLocaleString('pt-BR',{style:'currency',currency:'BRL'}) + '</span>', className:'text-right' }
    ],
    pageLength: 15,
    order: [[5,'desc']],
    language: {
      search: 'Buscar:', lengthMenu: 'Mostrar _MENU_', info: '_START_–_END_ de _TOTAL_',
      paginate: { next:'›', previous:'‹' }, zeroRecords: 'Nenhum resultado'
    }
  });

  document.querySelectorAll('#fase-filters .filter-btn').forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      document.querySelectorAll('#fase-filters .filter-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
      this.classList.add('active');
      currentFase = this.dataset.fase;
      if(currentFase === 'Todos') {
        dtTable.search('').columns(4).search('').draw();
      } else {
        dtTable.columns(4).search(currentFase).draw();
      }
    });
  });
}

// Render first page
renderPage('overview');
</script>
</body>
</html>
